
.. _AnyFunSetUnion:

##############
AnyFunSetUnion
##############

.. Do not edit this file.
.. It is automatically generated by ``reference/create_pages.py``

:Type: Abstract
:Parent class: :ref:`AnyFunInit`


**************
Description
**************


This is an abstract class implementing the function: :ref:`set_union()` .

.. seealso:: Please see the documentation on :ref:`set_union()` for more information
    on how to use the function.


.. Hack to insure that that an emtpy section deosn't screw
.. with the section levels.

|nbsp|







.. Do not edit this file.
.. Members are must be modified directly in the AMS source code.
